<script type="text/javascript">
  window._global_header_23_hit_exp_ = true;

  (function () {
    if (!window.localStorage || window.innerWidth < 1280) {
      return;
    }

    var spmb = document.body.getAttribute('data-spm');
    if (
      ['home', 'productlist', 'detail', 'categorymp', 'best'].indexOf(spmb) == -1 ||
      window._global_header_23_hit_exp_ != true
    ) {
      return;
    }

    function addClass(obj, cls) {
      if (!obj.className.match(new RegExp('(\\s|^)' + cls + '(\\s|$)'))) obj.className += ' ' + cls;
    }

    var statusStr = localStorage.getItem('sidecart_pre_status');
    var statusData;
    try {
      statusData = JSON.parse(statusStr);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
    if (['home', 'best'].indexOf(spmb) == -1 && statusData && statusData.show && statusData.time) {
      var minusTime = new Date().getTime() - statusData.time;
      if (minusTime < 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) {
        addClass(document.body, 'unfoldShopCart');
      }
    }
  })();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
(function () {
  var getCookie = (cookieKey) => {
    var cookies = document.cookie && document.cookie.split(';');
    for (var i = 0, length = cookies.length; i < length; i++) {
        var reg = new RegExp('^'+ cookieKey +'=');
        if (typeof cookies[i] === 'string' && reg.test(cookies[i].trim())) {
            return cookies[i];
        }
    }
  };
  if (/AliApp\(AE/.test(navigator.userAgent)) { return; }
  if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
    try {
      if (/(www|es|pt|fr|pl|ko|nl|it|de|tr|he|ja|ar|th|vi|id)\.aliexpress\.com/.test(window.location.host) || /www\.aliexpress\.us/.test(window.location.host)) {
        var version = /*!-->sw-data-start--*/'0.0.73/js'/*!-->sw-data-end--*/;
        navigator.serviceWorker
          .register('/sw.js?version='+version, {
            scope: '/',
          })
          .then((registration) => {
            if (registration.active) {
              registration.active.postMessage({
                type: 'sw_cookie_sync',
                data: ['aep_usuc_f', 'xman_us_f'].reduce((obj, key) => {
                  obj[key] = getCookie(key) || '';
                  return obj;
                }, {}),
              });
            }
          })
          .catch((err) => {
            console.error(err);
          });
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(e);
    }
  }
})();
</script></body></html>
